Synopsis:
Voice barks for Astarion as the player interacts with the screen. 'Normal' lines are lines spoken while walking about in the world, but not in combat or sneaking. 'Sneaking' lines are spoken while in stealth mode - crouched and hiding - and should be read in a hushed voice. 'Combat' lines are spoken while in combat, and should sound stressed/urgent unless otherwise indicated.

File E:\BG3_Unpack\Gustav_pak\Mods\Gustav\Story\Dialogs\Global\BG_PointAndClick\GLO_BG_PointNClick_Shadowheart_NarrativeArc_Start.lsj
Synopsis:
Point and click lines - assorted lines spoken by Shadowheart when the player engages her to do various actions or when she transitions between different states - her portrait is clicked upon in the UI, she starts to sneak, she's directed to interact with something or speak to someone. There's a large number of lines, many of which might be similar or identical - referring to the context field is particularly important as a result. IMPORTANT NOTE - in general, these lines should be considered as sotto voce or internal thoughts to herself. Though they sometimes are phrased as if addressing another character, they're not audible to others within the narrative - just SH and the player. Many phrases are similar or identical, in which case the specific context changes should be referred to.

Voice barks for Minthara as the player interacts with the screen. 'Normal' lines are lines spoken while walking about in the world, but not in combat or sneaking. 'Sneaking' lines are spoken while in stealth mode - crouched and hiding - and should be read in a hushed voice. 'Combat' lines are spoken while in combat, and should sound stressed/urgent unless otherwise indicated.

'Sneaking' lines are spoken while in stealth mode - crouched and hiding - and should be read in a hushed voice. 'Combat' lines are spoken while in combat, and should sound stressed/urgent unless otherwise indicated.
